DETECTOR   - Detector resolution: The energy resolutions of       E175600100029 
             measured neutron spectra are at maximum about 20%    E175600100030 
             for about 2000 MeV neutrons of highest energy at 0   E175600100031 
             degree and 7.5 degree, about 20% for about 1000 MeV  E175600100032 
             neutrons of highest energy at 15 degree and 30       E175600100033 
             degree, and about 40% for about 600 MeV neutrons of  E175600100034 
             highest energy at 60 degree and 90 degree, which     E175600100035 
             were produced by 800 MeV/nucleon Si ions.            E175600100036 
           - Calibration: Each E counter was calibrated with a    E175600100037 
             60Co Gamma-ray source.                               E175600100038 
           - Efficiency: The neutron detection efficiencies were  E175600100039 
             calculated with the Monte Carlo code of Cecil et al. E175600100040 
             for all energy ranges. Reference is R. A. Cecil, B.  E175600100041 
             D. Anderson, and R. Madey, Nucl. Instrum. Methods    E175600100042 
             161, 439 (1979).                                     E175600100043 
           (SCIN) Plastic scintillator (NE102A) was used as the   E175600100044 
                  delta-E counter and the beam pick-up counter.   E175600100045 
           (SCIN) Liquid scintillator (NE213) was used as the E   E175600100046 
                  counter.                                        E175600100047 
ERR-ANALYS The statistical uncertainties vary in a range of 2 to  E175600100048 
           5 % for the low- to medium-energy (5-400 MeV) region   E175600100049 
           of the spectra and increase to about 30% at the        E175600100050 
           highest energies.                                      E175600100051
